<script>
  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_bc757267-1570-46ab-a313-958f98fa27f6'
      });
    }
    
    var initializeSiwa = function() {
      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"
      loadScript(APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL, initAppleId);
    };
    if (typeof AppleID !== "undefined") {
      initAppleId();
    } else {
      initializeSiwa();
    }

</script>

<span id="freeTextContainer13679529772586543387"><b>Tensions rise, secrets grow bigger, and passions run deeper--and hotter--in Last Light, the second novel of the Night Owl Trilogy from bestselling author M. Pierce.</b><br/><br/>Matt Sky is missing.   <span id="freeText13679529772586543387" style="display:none"><b>Tensions rise, secrets grow bigger, and passions run deeper--and hotter--in Last Light, the second novel of the Night Owl Trilogy from bestselling author M. Pierce.</b><br /><br />Matt Sky is missing. After a solo ascent of Longs Peak that left only a large blood stain, tatters of climbing clothing, and the tracks of an animal in the snow, he is presumed dead.<br /><br />Hannah Catalano is guarding a secret: she knows Matt is alive. After Matt's memorial service, she lingers on the East Coast with his family, but it soon becomes clear that his brothers' motives are less than gracious. Nate Sky is bent on tracking down the author of Night Owl, a book that charts the last days of Matt's life with uncanny and scandalous accuracy, and which appeared only after his death. Seth Sky is bent on getting Hannah into his bed.<br /><br />Hidden away in the woods, Matt and Hannah strive desperately to maintain their ruse and their relationship--but their web of lies only tightens as Matt struggles with the consequences of his decision, and Hannah tries to escape Nate's libel suit and fend off Seth's advances...until Hannah is put in danger, and Matt must make a life or death choice.</span>
  <a data-text-id="13679529772586543387" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_764357412" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/764357412" />
    <a title="Patty ~ Wrapped Up In Reading Book Blog" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/14302918-patty-wrapped-up-in-reading-book-blog"><img alt="Patty ~ Wrapped Up In Reading Book Blog" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1518242765p2/14302918.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/764357412?book_show_action=true">Nov 13, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Patty ~ Wrapped Up In Reading Book Blog" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Patty ~ Wrapped Up In Reading Book Blog" href="/user/show/14302918-patty-wrapped-up-in-reading-book-blog">Patty ~ Wrapped Up In Reading Book Blog</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14302918-patty-wrapped-up-in-reading-book-blog?shelf=slightly-mental-book-boyfriend">slightly-mental-book-boyfriend</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14302918-patty-wrapped-up-in-reading-book-blog?shelf=panty-soaking-read">panty-soaking-read</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14302918-patty-wrapped-up-in-reading-book-blog?shelf=filthy-talking-book-boyfriend">filthy-talking-book-boyfriend</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer764357412" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11280490014346560203"><b>*****3.75 STARS*****</b><br/><br/><br/><a href='http://s1276.photobucket.com/user/tennyspa/media/bc19fa3aef687378dfdec61d259b6108_zps9b2129b1.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1414897766i/11702403._SY540_.jpg' alt=' photo bc19fa3aef687378dfdec61d259b6108_zps9b2129b1.jpg' width='365' height='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/><br/>It has been almost a year since I read the first book, <b>Night Owl</b>. I remembered how much I <b>LOVED</b> that book and how it brought a beautiful, filthy talking, and slightly peculiar book boyfriend into my life. I never forgot about Matt and his pet bunny, Laurence. I have been anxiously awaiting the release of <b>Last Light</b>. <br/><br/><br/><br/>I have to say, I'm not a fan of the <b>DNF</b> method, because I have found that many times a book that seems pretty dull in the first half, can somehow turn around </span>
  <span id="freeText11280490014346560203" style="display:none"><b>*****3.75 STARS*****</b><br><br><br><a href="http://s1276.photobucket.com/user/tennyspa/media/bc19fa3aef687378dfdec61d259b6108_zps9b2129b1.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1414897766i/11702403._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo bc19fa3aef687378dfdec61d259b6108_zps9b2129b1.jpg" width="365" height="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br>It has been almost a year since I read the first book, <b>Night Owl</b>. I remembered how much I <b>LOVED</b> that book and how it brought a beautiful, filthy talking, and slightly peculiar book boyfriend into my life. I never forgot about Matt and his pet bunny, Laurence. I have been anxiously awaiting the release of <b>Last Light</b>. <br><br><br><br>I have to say, I'm not a fan of the <b>DNF</b> method, because I have found that many times a book that seems pretty dull in the first half, can somehow turn around towards the end. This is what happened for me with <b>Last Light</b>. It took me <b>FIVE DAYS</b> to finish this book!! I did catch up on <b>a lot</b> of sleeping time while trying to read this one.<br><br><br><br>The story starts off with Matt faking his death to get away from the public eye. He was unable to handle all the attention from his fans. Matt missed his anonymity. Hannah is in on the secret and refuses to run off and start a new life with Matt. She doesn't want to leave her family or lose her career. So he holds up in a cabin in the mountains while Hannah still lives in their condo in Denver and goes about her life while playing along with the charade that Matt is truly dead. They see each other every weekend when she drives up to the cabin.<br><br><br>Hannah's reasons for not wanting to run away with Matt, make absolutely no sense! First off, she's an administrative assistant! She could get a job like that ANYWHERE!! ALSO, she HARDLY spent any time with her family. I was plenty annoyed with her. She kept harping on the fact that she thought Matt loved his writing more than her and that she didn't know him as well as people from his past knew him!! The dude almost killed himself over her in book one!! He has a constant hard on for her. I don't know...sounds like he's pretty crazy about her to me!!<br><br><br>Matt is keeping secrets and lying to Hannah again. In his slightly deranged mind, he thinks what he is doing will convince Hannah to leave her life in Denver behind and run off with him instead.<br><br><br>I think because for most of the book these two were separated, it just felt off to me. Matt didn't seem as odd as he did in the first book. I missed his craziness. Maybe he needed his pet bunny with him!! The sex in the first half seemed a bit tame and rushed.<br><br><br><br>BUT, then towards the last 40% of the book, the story starts to get interesting. There are a couple of characters that will try to get between the two lovers. I started to feel the angst. There is something that Hannah does that I wish the author just completely left out of the book. <br><br><br><br>Truths are revealed, which forces Matt out of hiding and when he and Hannah come together, the sex is finally <b>HOT</b>!!! I started to have hope that I would end up liking the book after all. Matt actually became swoonworthy again!! <br><br><br><a href="http://s1276.photobucket.com/user/tennyspa/media/616137_zpsecvyh5g8.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1414897766ra/11702404.gif" alt=" photo 616137_zpsecvyh5g8.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br>I can safely say that I did end up liking the book. Was it better than the first? No. But it was enjoyable towards the end. It ends on a little cliffy. Nothing bad. I promise. Will I read <b>After Dark</b> when it comes out? YES!<br>I want to see what happens next for Matt, and his "little bird".</span>
  <a data-text-id="11280490014346560203" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_755425584" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/755425584" />
    <a title="Michelle" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/13126896-michelle"><img alt="Michelle" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1505605297p2/13126896.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/755425584?book_show_action=true">Nov 03, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Michelle" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Michelle" href="/user/show/13126896-michelle">Michelle</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer755425584" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6068866770571913707">In the follow up to Night Owl, M. Pierce brings us Last Light. Now after that epilogue in NO and all the speculation that swirled around how a trilogy was going to be created following that ending. <br/><br/>Matthew loved three things. Writing, his privacy and Hannah. Last Light is the discover of just what one of those things he loved more and what things he’d be willing to give up in order to have them. Matt wanted to fade away into the back ground, but with his identity known, that was no longer possib</span>
  <span id="freeText6068866770571913707" style="display:none">In the follow up to Night Owl, M. Pierce brings us Last Light. Now after that epilogue in NO and all the speculation that swirled around how a trilogy was going to be created following that ending. <br><br>Matthew loved three things. Writing, his privacy and Hannah. Last Light is the discover of just what one of those things he loved more and what things he’d be willing to give up in order to have them. Matt wanted to fade away into the back ground, but with his identity known, that was no longer possible. After news of his death makes the news, a story appears. Not just any story. Matt &amp; Hannah’s story. In all its glory. Every explicit detail. But how did it end up online? Who stole the story to publish?<br><br>Hannah knew she loved Matt. She knew she’d do anything to help him, even if that meant that he was taken away from her. As she carries on the lie, she is forced having to face Nate and his drive to restore the legacy to Matt’s writing by unearthing the person behind Night Owl and Seth, the other Sky brother seems to want to stop at nothing while pursing the woman that fell for his brother. <br><br>Things get a bit more complicated as more lies are told and the truth unfolds. <br><br>Can I just say that I loved Night Owl? And that I am so pleased that this did not get turned into a Paranormal Romance. So that out of the way, I struggled with some of the aspects of this story until the very end. The addition of Seth to this story along with the little secret that Matt was keeping from Hannah made me all kinds of uncomfortable. For about 60% of the book I felt like due to the way Night Owl ended, that this story was sort of painted into a corner and getting out of that was going to be painful. As much as the way things in Night Owl had no impact on me <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ his cheating <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>, there was something much different in this book. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ As much as cheating never really bothered me in Night Owl, the way Hannah was with Seth and Matt with Mel... it just pissed me off. I was nearly ready to just put it down at one point because I was struggling so hard with the direction of this story.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br>Once I got to the point in the story where some hard choices, I found myself pulled back in. There was far more story to this installment, it wasn’t just about the hot sex and asshole personality of Matt. Where Night Owl focused on the coupling of these two, Last Light gave you the story. The words and actions to move this series along to the final installment. <br><br>I wasn’t sure what I wanted when it came to this story. Part of me wanted the same feelings that Night Owl evoked, but I needed a story. It wasn’t until the end of this that it all came together, but I do feel like I walk away from this book with less feeling for Matt &amp; Hannah that I originally had going into it. <br><br>M. Pierce has a lot to live up to after delivering such an amazing debut with Night Owl. I am interested to see the response to this novel from readers. I was very pleased with the story by the time I read the last few lines and am back to feeling that same excitement for the release of the conclusion of this trilogy. <br><br><i> Images to be added soon. </i><br><br><br><a href="https://www.flickr.com/photos/125438022@N06/15250834182" title="ARC by Book Worm, on Flickr" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1410813673i/11155676.jpg" width="400" height="166" alt="ARC" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Lise *friends don&#39;t flag*" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Lise *friends don&#39;t flag*" href="/user/show/8191340-lise-friends-don-t-flag">Lise *friends don&#39;t flag*</a>

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8191340-lise-friends-don-t-flag?shelf=steamy">steamy</a>,

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8191340-lise-friends-don-t-flag?shelf=arc">arc</a>,

          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer755607955" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16726316764990340617"><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1413131342ra/11469478.gif' width='400' height='250' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Night Owl was a favorite read of mine so when I saw book two up on Netgalley I was a requesting fool and was shocked to be so lucky to receive an arc…<br/><br/>I enjoyed book two in this three part series, perhaps not as much as book one but I still loved it. I loved being in Matt’s crazy thinking head while he is plotting and lying and loving on his “little bird”- Hannah.<br/><br/>What seemed to Matt to be a perfect way of gaining his privacy back and have Hannah all to himself, is turning into a bit of the opposi</span>
  <span id="freeText16726316764990340617" style="display:none"><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1413131342ra/11469478.gif" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Night Owl was a favorite read of mine so when I saw book two up on Netgalley I was a requesting fool and was shocked to be so lucky to receive an arc…<br><br>I enjoyed book two in this three part series, perhaps not as much as book one but I still loved it. I loved being in Matt’s crazy thinking head while he is plotting and lying and loving on his “little bird”- Hannah.<br><br>What seemed to Matt to be a perfect way of gaining his privacy back and have Hannah all to himself, is turning into a bit of the opposite as Matt and Hannah can only be together on weekends and in secret. <br><br>Matt lives for his weekend rendezvous’ with Hannah and busies himself with his writing and reasoning. <br><br>Hannah is continuing with her work during the week and then weekends with Matt. She is still trying to get to know Matt on a deeper level and he is just not willing or ready to share. However, with Sky brothers, Nate and Seth popping up here and there- Hannah is finding out some interesting things about Matt. <br><br>The connection between Matt and Hannah is so intense and all consuming and when they are together- on top of each other-inside one another… I can’t get enough of their dirty talking, position changing, turn me on like a beacon ways…*sigh*<br><br>But is this physical perfection enough for them to last one more <i>“last light” of day?</i> Will the lies and secrets they are keeping from one another cause a downward spiral of misery and hurt? Will they fall into the arms of others?<br><br>Oh… my Matt Sky, M. Pierce loving friends… just wait until you get your hands on this one. It will make you crazy and seek comfort by-<br> <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1413580424ra/11531916.gif" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b>petting an owl of course</b><br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br></span>

<div id="review_753833462" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/753833462" />
    <a title="AJ" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3143126-aj"><img alt="AJ" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1406382884p2/3143126.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/753833462?book_show_action=true">Oct 31, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="AJ" class="user" itemprop="url" name="AJ" href="/user/show/3143126-aj">AJ</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=arc">arc</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=steamy">steamy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=series">series</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=celebrity">celebrity</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=romantic">romantic</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer753833462" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer730974919085986913"><b><i>Everything was so fucked-up. So many lies. A castle of lies. And Matt was its king, and I was the queen, holding together our elaborate deception.</i><br/><br/>3 sadly underwhelming stars</b><br/><br/>I’m gutted to be writing this review right now. After the stunningly surprising introduction to this series with <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/20646604.Night_Owl__Night_Owl___1_' title='Night Owl (Night Owl, #1) by M. Pierce' rel='nofollow noopener'>Night Owl</a>, my expectations were high, and I was beyond excited to read the continuation of Matt and Hannah’s story. But I actually found this book quite boring, and I had a couple of issues with some of the behavio</span>
  <span id="freeText730974919085986913" style="display:none"><b><i>Everything was so fucked-up. So many lies. A castle of lies. And Matt was its king, and I was the queen, holding together our elaborate deception.</i><br /><br />3 sadly underwhelming stars</b><br /><br />I’m gutted to be writing this review right now. After the stunningly surprising introduction to this series with <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/20646604.Night_Owl__Night_Owl___1_" title="Night Owl (Night Owl, #1) by M. Pierce" rel="nofollow noopener">Night Owl</a>, my expectations were high, and I was beyond excited to read the continuation of Matt and Hannah’s story. But I actually found this book quite boring, and I had a couple of issues with some of the behaviour going on. <br /><br /><i>Last Light</i> picks up right after the end of that ‘WTF?’ epilogue at the end of <i>Night Owl</i> - and please be warned that this review will contain spoilers for that book. <br /><br />To the outside world, Matt is dead. Although he is secretly living in a cabin in the woods in order to finally find privacy and escape from the constant public scrutiny that he struggles with so much. So while he lives his life in hiding, he broods, he writes, and he thinks about Hannah. <br /><br />Hannah is in on Matt's big secret, but with too many ties in her life to disappear with him, she is living the life of the shattered girlfriend, keeping up the façade to friends and family while she counts down the days until she can sneak off and see him again. <br /><br />Matt and Hannah’s obsession for each other is still very much present, but it’s mixed in with a deep love, and the intensity of their relationship and their passion for each other is all consuming. The daydreams, telephone calls and phone sex help tide them over but they only go so far, which makes their reunions a little bit epic, and when they are able to be together, it is hot, intense, a little bit kinky and dirty as all hell. <br /><br /><blockquote>
  <i>Absence doesn’t make the heart go yonder or grow fonder. Absence makes people horny as fuck.</i>
</blockquote><br />Bringing a touch of drama to the story is the internet release of Night Owl – Matt’s book chronicling his relationship with Hannah – in extremely explicit, smutty detail. With Matt presumed dead, speculation is rife over who wrote the book, and who actually released it, and Hannah is left to deal with the fallout of her private life being exposed to all. <br /><br />I loved the inclusion of Matt's brothers in the story! Big brother, Nate is there to support Hannah and help her cope with all that she is facing, and then Matt’s other brother, Seth comes into the picture. Sexy, arrogant and openly flirty with Hannah, his presence in her life only adds to her confusion. <br /><br />I loved <i>Night Owl</i>. Seriously loved it! It was different, it was shocking, and it was full of emotion. Sadly, this book didn’t hit me as hard, and I was bored for most of it because there’s not a lot going on in the story.<br /><br />I had heard that M. Pierce’s original intention was for this book to shift the series into a minor paranormal setting, then he got a publishing deal and was asked to keep it contemporary. I’m not sure where he was going to take the story, but I feel like an opportunity has been missed here. For an author to be asked to change his entire concept for his series just seems wrong to me. I’m not sure if that’s the reason why this book lacked the intensity of the first, but it seemed a little directionless, just meandering through some drama for the sake of drama. I still really like his writing style, and he told the story well, there just wasn’t enough of it.<br /><br />And when I say drama, the whole lot of it could have been easily avoided. There is stupid behaviour from both of them. Matt shows his secretive, manipulative side, and even though I like his unique craziness, he really went too far in this one. And Hannah’s stupid just pissed me off. And the whole way through, there are just too many lies!<br /><br /><blockquote><i>Why did I always do the worst things? Why did I always arrange my life so that is was on the brink of collapse?<br />The answer came to me as if it had only been waiting for the question.<br /></i>Because happiness is useless to me. Because I need agony and heat in my life.<i><br />I swallowed. My saliva was bitter. </i></blockquote><br />The book does end on a (somewhat hastily reached) good point, with no cliffhanger - although it's definitely left open. And even though I have no idea what is going to happen in the next book, I’m curious enough to pick it up to see how Matt and Hannah finish out the series. <br /><br />I really wanted to love this one, but I just didn’t feel it as much as I wanted to. 3 stars.<br /><br /><br /><i>An Advanced Reader Copy of this book was generously provided by the publisher in exchange for an honest review.</i><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="730974919085986913" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ " href="/user/show/3275325-sharon-is-an-emotional-book-junkie">Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ </a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer762662388" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer14234919592515942499">3.5 - 4 ★'s <br/><br/>It's been a long journey just getting to this book. With the author going from self published to having a publisher and the inevitable release delay. Add to that the change of plot from a possible paranormal twist to keeping it just contemporary, well, I was a bit overwhelmed with all the possibilities. Unfortunately, after reading, I'm left feeling a bit <b>
  <i>under</i>
</b>whelmed!<br/><br/>Hopefully, you've read the first book and you know that Matt has some issues. Yes, he's handsome, a dirty talker </span>
  <span id="freeText14234919592515942499" style="display:none">3.5 - 4 ★'s <br><br>It's been a long journey just getting to this book. With the author going from self published to having a publisher and the inevitable release delay. Add to that the change of plot from a possible paranormal twist to keeping it just contemporary, well, I was a bit overwhelmed with all the possibilities. Unfortunately, after reading, I'm left feeling a bit <b>
  <i>under</i>
</b>whelmed!<br><br>Hopefully, you've read the first book and you know that Matt has some issues. Yes, he's handsome, a dirty talker and quite sexually intense but he's also a liar, addict and a manipulator. He can be paranoid and he treasures his privacy but how did he get to this point? We've gotten a few tidbits but...I <i>need</i> to know why he's this way. <br><br>And as always, it just seems that poor Hannah is barely hanging on for the ride. She's been totally consumed by Matt. But thank goodness, she has some moments of clarity and hopefully it's enough for Matt to make a <i>real</i> effort in changing. <br><br>So Matt came up with a plan, executed it and basically forced Hannah to go along with things. Things she's not too happy about. In fact, some things were hard to read because really she's floundering...and it only gets worse. <br><br>Throw in some really weird and awkward plot twists and you really have to question why. What were the reasonings for Seth and Melanie? I hated the direction the story took with them and really the only thing I can think of is what came from it. Maybe this will be something that will be explained in the next book...or maybe not. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1413693191i/11548076.jpg" width="300" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Regardless, you will be happy to know that the book is still as steamy as ever! Matt and Hannah go at it often and just about anywhere and anytime. Throw in some toys, some role play, the ever increasing BDSM influences, some back door luvins' and there you go. <br><br>I'm thankful we had both their POVs...I think things would have been a mess without it. In a way, I can see where Matt was coming from with all his lies and manipulations but I feel as though he didn't learn anything. And my mind is boggled by what Hannah did at the end (sorry I can't say...it's a BIG spoiler) especially when I like all her other stipulations. <br><br>So I have no clue what the next book will be about. Clearly, things will move forward but unless Matt really turns a corner, things are gonna be messy. And could the title be any more ambiguous? <i>After Dark</i>....whatttt??<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1415484871i/11798054.jpg" width="400" height="125" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b>
  <u>Favorite quotes:</u>
</b><br><br>♥ "The heart always knows what the mind refuses to accept."<br><br>♥ "Do we have room for all my animal friends?"<br><br>♥ “Let’s not live like other people. Let’s not be like other couples.” <br><br>♥ “Because happiness is useless to me. Because I need agony and heat in my life.”</span>

<span id="freeTextContainer15089180491462164415"><b>Lies!</b> So many <i>lies</i> ... <br/><blockquote>
<b><i>We'd been here before, and because of my lies.<br/>Happiness is useless to me.</i></b><br/><br/>It took me a long time to pick up this book. Perhaps because I loved <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/20646604.Night_Owl__Night_Owl___1_' title='Night Owl (Night Owl, #1) by M. Pierce' rel='nofollow noopener'>Night Owl</a> so immensely ... I was quite certain that this wouldn't live up to my expectations. And, while this one didn't quite elicit the same intense feelings that I had for the first, it was certainly not a letdown. In fact, I was pleasantly surprised at how much I enjoyed it. And how much I missed <b>Matt</b> ...<br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1425749869i/13927900._SX540_.jpg' width='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>Oh.Em.Gee! I frekin' LOV</b></blockquote></span>
  <span id="freeText15089180491462164415" style="display:none"><b>Lies!</b> So many <i>lies</i> ... <br><blockquote>

Pierce" rel="nofollow noopener">Night Owl</a> so immensely ... I was quite certain that this wouldn't live up to my expectations. I frekin' LOVE Matthew Sky!</b><br>Such a filthy talking, shameless, tortured, artistic and overall amazingly flawed character. If he was real ... well, I'd be camping out on his doorstep. It was Hannah that surprised me the most in this one ... she took on a new dimension in this story.<br><blockquote><b><i>With our black-eyed reflections and love-marked bodies, we looked criminal.<br>...   <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/755182414" />

  <div class="left bodycol">

        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/755182414?book_show_action=true">Nov 02, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Amy J Romance Author &amp; Reader Events" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Amy J Romance Author &amp; Reader Events" href="/user/show/9164629-amy-j-romance-author-reader-events">Amy J Romance Author &amp; Reader Events</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9164629-amy-j-romance-author-reader-events?shelf=angsty">angsty</a>,

              <span id="reviewTextContainer755182414" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer13278994600858023296">ARC PROVIDED FOR HONEST REVIEW<br/>5 ***** Narcissistic Schizo Steamy Hot Stars*****<br/><br/>I know this makes absolutely no freaking sense...<br/><br/>So you know when you read a book until the wee hours of the night? You flip that last page and then there is just so much to say? So much to think? So much to share? AND NO ONE is around to discuss! Just you and the glow of your kindle illuminating the dark recesses of your room as you frantically type an emotionally filled review scouring your highlights and notes. The</span>
  <span id="freeText13278994600858023296" style="display:none">ARC PROVIDED FOR HONEST REVIEW<br>5 ***** Narcissistic Schizo Steamy Hot Stars*****<br><br>I know this makes absolutely no freaking sense...<br><br>So you know when you read a book until the wee hours of the night? You flip that last page and then there is just so much to say? So much to think? So much to share? AND NO ONE is around to discuss! Just you and the glow of your kindle illuminating the dark recesses of your room as you frantically type an emotionally filled review scouring your highlights and notes. Then I realized, there is NOTHING to write in my review. Everything, I mean everything would give something away and I don't want to taint your genuine reactions. As much as we all love the dysfunctional Matt Sky and M. Pierce you will love them even more after this book, well most of you will. BUT , you will ADORE Hannah more than ever.<br><br>Second books in a series are usually difficult for me to enjoy. They just don't seem to live up to the first and don't end quite yet so were often left in the "middle" of some conflict or left hanging for our closure with the characters. At first I thought here we go again another mehhh second book but then I realized I was feeling exactly what M wanted me to feel. Damn him! He cleans the slate in your mind of preconceived notions and has you reeling as a spectator to Hurricane Matt. In my notes section I wrote the following terms of endearment while reading , and in no particular order: A**, narcissistic douche, entitled, manipulative, hypocrite, paranoid, and schizo-you know, all the reasons we fell in love with him in Night Owl.<br><br>Yes, he did it AGAIN....its another hit. M has successfully pulled in many fans to his plausible reality by writing with such emotion and personal investment (or so it seems) that we all feel like were "friends" , we know him, were LOYAL to him. We all believe we are part of his world real or not.<br><br>It goes without saying, there are some hot steamy scenes and THANK YOU JESUS cause no one writes hot like M. **Warning the 65% mark is smoldering (and my favorite) ** OK well there is one other but you get the point.<br><br>Now I know why the blurb is so short or now looking at it I'm thinking vague. Is there nothing M. Pierce does without purpose? Is this story true or real? Is M purposely walking the fine line of reality and fiction or just making us think he is? The writing flow and story intertwined with plausible reality = marketing genius. <br><br>Like I said, there isn't much to say without giving away spoilers so I leave you with some quotes and emotions.<br><b> <i><br>"We weren't so different in our desires"<br>"Dangerous...these changeable moods"<br>"The heart always knows what the mind refuses to accept"<br>"Effing Sky men with their presumptuous stares"<br>"Ecstasy is a strange fire"<br>"Unless your name is Hannah this is a no a** shaking zone"</i></b><br><br>There are so many more I have highlighted but they will give too much away!<br><br><a href="http://s1340.photobucket.com/user/amy_jennings2/media/tumblr_mheqkagOpf1qihp55o1_250_zps92552413.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1413051532ra/11460202.gif" alt="oops photo tumblr_mheqkagOpf1qihp55o1_250_zps92552413.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><a href="http://s1340.photobucket.com/user/amy_jennings2/media/wtf_zps54c389f4.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1413051532i/11460203.jpg" alt=" photo wtf_zps54c389f4.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><a href="http://s1340.photobucket.com/user/amy_jennings2/media/6101649_zps990364ee.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

<span id="freeTextContainer15454741065659387416"><b>4 Bird Love Stars!!</b><br/><br/><b>Casting:</b><br/><a href='http://s996.photobucket.com/user/Vanessa_RB-Babe/media/LastlightCasting_zps1dc24b74.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1415286434i/11764890.jpg' alt=' photo LastlightCasting_zps1dc24b74.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><i>I know that Jamie Dornan is forever going to by type-casted as Christian Grey but to me, he is the perfect Matt Sky too! I have always envisioned him as this character. He's got that whole tortured , sexy, brooding thing going on that is such a huge part of Matt's personality!</i><br/><br/>Aww, well, I didn't love it as much as <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/20646604.Night_Owl__Night_Owl___1_' title='Night Owl (Night Owl, #1) by M. Pierce' rel='nofollow noopener'>Night Owl</a> but it was still pretty great. The pacing was a tiny bit slow for me in the beginning but once it got going, I was hooked. The tone felt a bit </span>
  <span id="freeText15454741065659387416" style="display:none"><b>4 Bird Love Stars!!</b><br><br><b>Casting:</b><br><a href="http://s996.photobucket.com/user/Vanessa_RB-Babe/media/LastlightCasting_zps1dc24b74.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1415286434i/11764890.jpg" alt=" photo LastlightCasting_zps1dc24b74.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><i>I know that Jamie Dornan is forever going to by type-casted as Christian Grey but to me, he is the perfect Matt Sky too! I have always envisioned him as this character. He's got that whole tortured , sexy, brooding thing going on that is such a huge part of Matt's personality!</i><br><br>Aww, well, I didn't love it as much as <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/20646604.Night_Owl__Night_Owl___1_" title="Night Owl (Night Owl, #1) by M. Pierce" rel="nofollow noopener">Night Owl</a> but it was still pretty great. The pacing was a tiny bit slow for me in the beginning but once it got going, I was hooked. The tone felt a bit depressing to me at first too, but after reading the blurb for the third book, I think this part of the second book was supposed to feel that way. And, it didn't last long. <br><br>Matt is still one of my very fave book boyfriends. I love his snarky, pissy humor and general outlook on life. You can't help but laugh at him, even when he's at his most arrogant. Hannah will forever be Matt's muse. It's his way of trying to process her impact on his life. And Hannah takes the cake in her strength and determination when it comes to their relationship. External factors continue to threaten these two. They're better, but they still have their issues to work out. Some decisions that BOTH of them made, could have easily irked me, but they felt very real and believable for these characters and where they are at right now. For all those fans (like me) of messy Matt, who is very rough around the edges, fret not, he's a little better, but he's still making his mistakes and figuring stuff out. I won't say more but just know that this is a fun and intense read....oh yeah, and these two are still just as hot and heavy as ever, and Matt's mouth is still just as filthy!!! <br><br>Like, seriously... <br><b>**WARNING - R Rated Teaser up ahead**</b><br><br><b>
  <i>"When I fuck you ... I love to watch your breasts tremble." I bit her neck. She shuddered. "When I hit your ass ... I love to watch it quiver. I love your name. I love to moan it. You know I moan your name when I jerk off alone. Hannah... Hannah..."</i>
</b> And that is just a taste!! Soooo much more in this book!! <br><br>And some PG favorites...<br><br><b>
  <i>"I'm sorry I keep writing about you. I keep thinking about you. I'm obsessed with you."</i>
</b>- Matt <br><br><b>
  <i>"I don't want to be the sun in your sky," she continued. "Do you get what I mean? I'm happy being the moon. I'm happy coming second to your writing. If this crazy thing we're going to do is what it takes to protect your first love, then I'm game. We're in this together, Matt. You can count on me."</i>
</b> - Hannah<br><br>Oh, and to the supporting characters: <br><br><b>Nate -</b> I love you! What a great brother. Every scene with him just made me smile. <br><b>Seth -</b> You creep me out dude.. even if you sing. Just..go away! Bro code...ever heard of it? Piss me off! <br><b>Melanie -</b> Just....no. Go back to whatever freak, fan-girl rock you climbed out from under and stay there!! (Although, the one scene with her, did crack me up! I can't quote it, b/c it's a spoiler. You'll know when you get to it though.) <br><br>My favorite element of these books is still the quality of the writing. I don't know or care if M. Pierce is a guy, a girl, or a duo of both but damn....he/she/they can damn write!! <br><br>I loved this quote ---&gt; <b>
  <i>"...but the world is full of beautiful women, and love, which starts as a feeling, but ends as a choice."</i>
</b> That one stuck with me. <br><br>Can't wait for the third book!!! </span>

<div id="review_756229232" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/756229232" />
    <a title="Brenna" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/12928663-brenna"><img alt="Brenna" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1580475762p2/12928663.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/756229232?book_show_action=true">Nov 03, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Brenna" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Brenna" href="/user/show/12928663-brenna">Brenna</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12928663-brenna?shelf=arc">arc</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12928663-brenna?shelf=loveable-jerk">loveable-jerk</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12928663-brenna?shelf=romantic">romantic</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12928663-brenna?shelf=series">series</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12928663-brenna?shelf=erotica">erotica</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer756229232" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10690837437568465963"><i>
  <b>“I’m sorry I keep writing about you. I keep thinking about you. I’m obsessed with you.”</b>
</i><br/><br/><i>Night Owl</i> was one of my favorite reads of 2013 so it pretty much goes without saying that I have been anxiously awaiting the release of <i>Last Light</i> all year. While I enjoyed this one, it didn’t quite live up to the amazing feeling I got from the first book. <br/><br/>After the shocking epilogue in <i>Night Owl</i>, I knew this was going to be a crazy ride with Matt and Hannah. Matt, unable to handle the public scrutiny and </span>
  <span id="freeText10690837437568465963" style="display:none"><i>
  <b>“I’m sorry I keep writing about you. I keep thinking about you. I’m obsessed with you.”</b>
</i><br /><br /><i>Night Owl</i> was one of my favorite reads of 2013 so it pretty much goes without saying that I have been anxiously awaiting the release of <i>Last Light</i> all year. While I enjoyed this one, it didn’t quite live up to the amazing feeling I got from the first book. <br /><br />After the shocking epilogue in <i>Night Owl</i>, I knew this was going to be a crazy ride with Matt and Hannah. Matt, unable to handle the public scrutiny and lack of privacy from being outed as author M. Pierce, fakes his death. Hannah, who is complicit in this plan is left to deal with his grieving family, an e-book scandal recounting all the sordid details of their love life, and Matt’s crazier than ever behavior. <br /><i>
  <blockquote>She would understand how cruel the media can be. She would fear the public, with its vulgar curiosity and sickening sense of entitlement.<br />And then she would come to me.</blockquote>
</i><br />While hiding out in the mountains of Colorado, Matt and Hannah are resigned to infrequent phone calls and the occasional weekend visit. While Hannah feels like his partner in crime, the only one knowing he’s alive, Matt is actually keeping secrets from her that could ruin everything. There is a lot of lying, half truths and manipulation going on and at times I wanted to scream at them to just tell the truth!<br /><i>
  <blockquote>When would it be my turn to truly know him? <br />Fear answered: Never. You’ll never know him. You can’t hold a man like that.</blockquote>
</i><br />There were definitely some things that didn’t work for me, but also a lot I loved about his book. For one, the writing. I am a huge fan of M. Pierce’s writing style and its easy flow. I liked that the characters <i>felt</i> the same to me, yes there were changes, but it was easy to pick this up and remember how I loved them <i>Night Owl</i>. There is quite a bit of time with Matt’s brother Nate and the addition of the middle brother, Seth. Seth brings in a bit of mystery and a little drama, which at times I loved and other I didn’t. Either way, I liked him as a character and found myself really intrigued by his part in the story. Matt is just as filthy as ever, with many sex scenes including his embarrassing style of kinky fuckery and dirty talk. I actually like the sex scenes for their originality and I can’t help but be shocked by the things that come out of Matt’s mouth, they are at times hilarious and also kind of disgusting - ha!<br /><br />I would have liked if the story was a little faster moving because for a majority of the book I kept asking myself, “where is this going!?” and wondering when something big would happen. It ended up being a bit boring at times and if it wasn’t for the strong character that Matt is, I think I would have struggled. My expectations may have been too high after just how much I loved <i>Night Owl</i>, but this one just didn’t have the same feel of excitement. All that said, I really am looking forward to the conclusion of the trilogy because I do love Matt and Hannah’s crazy dysfunction, even if it is at times a little over the top. <br /><br /><b>3.5 stars.</b><br /><br /><i>ARC kindly provided by St. Martin's Press via NetGalley in exchange for an honest review.</i><br /></span>

<div id="review_753889090" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/753889090" />
    <a title="Kayla at MyBookMuse" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/10212063-kayla-at-mybookmuse"><img alt="Kayla at MyBookMuse" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1412025796p2/10212063.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/753889090?book_show_action=true">Oct 31, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Kayla at MyBookMuse" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Kayla at MyBookMuse" href="/user/show/10212063-kayla-at-mybookmuse">Kayla at MyBookMuse</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer753889090" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3626237141550672546">"I don't want to be the sun in your sky," she continued. "Do you get what I mean? I'm happy coming second to your writing. I don't want to be your whole life. And if this–If this crazy thing we're going to do is what it takes to protect your first love, then I'm game. We're in this together, Matt. You can count on me."<br/><br/>There will be slight spoilers in this review. While I will clearly put the bigger ones in spoiler tags some details will be discussed that you might find spoiler-ish. Read at your </span>
  <span id="freeText3626237141550672546" style="display:none">"I don't want to be the sun in your sky," she continued. "Do you get what I mean? I'm happy coming second to your writing. I don't want to be your whole life. And if this–If this crazy thing we're going to do is what it takes to protect your first love, then I'm game. We're in this together, Matt. You can count on me."<br /><br />There will be slight spoilers in this review. While I will clearly put the bigger ones in spoiler tags some details will be discussed that you might find spoiler-ish. Read at your own risk...<br /><br />I honestly don't know how I feel about the second installment of The Night Owl Trilogy. There are a few things I liked but the overall feeling I had was underwhelmed and really put off. For example, one of the things I loved about this story was the drama. Matt and Hannah are on the angst-express and rounding the corner at 100mph. On the other hand, one of the things I hated was the drama. Like the kind that feels like angst for the sake of angst. Kind of a double-edged sword there, huh? Let me explain...<br /><br />"Matt loved to see me desperate for him; I loved to see him desperate for me. We weren't so different in our desires."<br /><br />Last Light starts off with Matt and Hannah dealing with the fall-out of Matt's identity being discovered. Matt has always valued his privacy, so this is something that he cannot come to terms with. Matt, being the ever irrational man that he is, decides that faking his death is the only way to escape his unwanted fame. Hannah goes along with this and helps him concoct a believable story and this sets into motion a series of events that tests the strength and commitment of their relationship. One of the events that takes places after Matt's planned demise is the discovery of a tell-all book being released that details the highly sexual and sensitive nature of Hannah and Matt's relationship. Hannah is devastated by her dirty laundry being public fodder in the wake of Matt's "death" and with the help of Matt's brother, they are out to discover who could possibly be the culprit of this huge invasion of privacy. Unbeknownst to Hannah <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ Matt is the actual writer of the tell-all and after finding another writer through the same forums that he and Hannah met, he has her release it under a pen name. His motivation for doing this is so that Hannah will be so embarrassed that she will leave her life to go live in the mountains, in seclusion, with him. For one, that is HIGHLY juvenile and really puts a bad taste in my mouth. Matt is no choir boy, but you would think that his character would have developed instead of regressed.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br />"A moment ago, he was convincing in his force. Now he was convincing in his gentle concern. I didn't ask myself which was the real Matt. People are light and dark."<br /><br />Because of that particular part of the story <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Matt starts a "working" relationship with the writer, Mel, who published the story and it blurs the lines of cheating. Not only does he pay this writer to come be his chauffeur during the week while Hannah is working, but one particular incident leaves Mel coming on to Matt. I don't take issue to cheating, and I'm sure many people would take issue with me calling it that, but Mel clearly hits on Matt and then grabs his dick, climbs on top of him, and proceeds to stick her tongue down his throat. Matt of course tells her off, but the whole interaction was just so wrong. While I give credit to M. Pierce for not sugar coating the situation and for example write Matt off as one of those characters that can only get hard for his girlfriend, she clearly went the controversial route and Matt is turned on and ponders what would happen if he did decide to start something with Mel.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> Not only is this really upsetting but it felt like Matt was just repeating history <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ like how he started messing around with Hannah while he was still with someone.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> But my biggest problem with Last Light deals with the fact that <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Matt's super creepy brother, Seth, tries to come on to Hannah repeatedly throughout the book. When Hanna and Matt break up, Hannah goes to Seth's hotel room and gives him a handjob. Sure, that isn't cheating but it's his brother. It just crossed a line that grossed me out.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>. So overall I was really put-off by a lot in this book. Matt and Hannah were destructive together and I don't see how they could possibly ever have a functional relationship. Will I continue the series? Yes. I believe there will be more character growth in the last book and I'm very curious to see how it plays out. For fans of the series, this is one of those books that really pushes you out of your comfort zone and that may or may not be a good thing.</span>

<div id="review_1083469373" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1083469373" />
    <a title="~Stéphanie&#39;s Journal~" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/24323583-st-phanie-s-journal"><img alt="~Stéphanie&#39;s Journal~" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1567153083p2/24323583.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1083469373?book_show_action=true">Oct 18, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="~Stéphanie&#39;s Journal~" class="user" itemprop="url" name="~Stéphanie&#39;s Journal~" href="/user/show/24323583-st-phanie-s-journal">~Stéphanie&#39;s Journal~</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/24323583-st-phanie-s-journal?shelf=buddy-read">buddy-read</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1083469373" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4369073499534406278">Before writing my review I re-read my review for Night Owl and I have to laugh because I'm in the exact same position I was two weeks ago!<br/><br/>I feel like I need to separate what I feel while reading the book and what I think about it.<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1415031782ra/11718456.gif' width='400' height='112' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>My problem is Matt and how he is or how he acts. In the first book, I knew he had problems, as I said in my first review, he's secretive to an extreme. I understand that as a lot of artist, he's a tormented soul. The thing is, why is he so tortured? I would really like </span>
  <span id="freeText4369073499534406278" style="display:none">Before writing my review I re-read my review for Night Owl and I have to laugh because I'm in the exact same position I was two weeks ago!<br><br>I feel like I need to separate what I feel while reading the book and what I think about it.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1415031782ra/11718456.gif" width="400" height="112" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>My problem is Matt and how he is or how he acts. In the first book, I knew he had problems, as I said in my first review, he's secretive to an extreme. I understand that as a lot of artist, he's a tormented soul. The thing is, why is he so tortured? I would really like to have my answer because I think that Matt lived past events which push him to act the way he does.<br>I can understand his need for privacy, it's his choice and I can accept that even M.Pierce the author doesn't share much about him/herself but for Matt, IMO, it goes too far.<br><br><b>What the story is all about?</b><br><br>The story begins with Matt who fakes death with everyone (his family, his friends, his agent), only Hannah knows the truth. And so the story will be based on how she handle Matt's disappearance and her interactions with others. How her relationship with Matt is going to be affected? How will she manage to lie to Nate, Matt 's brother? At Pam Matt 's agent whose also Hannah's employer? In this book, you'll also meet new characters that are going to complicate the relationship between Matt and Hannah ... although Matt takes care of the complicated side alone! <br><br><b>My feelings</b><br><br>It's difficult to put into words how/what I feel. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1415031977ra/11718466.gif" width="400" height="230" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>For most of the book, I was angry. First, against Hannah because I didn't understand her love for Matt. She's with him for months and she knows so little about him that I don't understand why she stays with him. For me she accepts too easily how he is.<br> <blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>Because I felt responsible for his unhappiness</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br>I don't speak of changing him but when you live with somebody, it's natural to know his secrets, his past, to understand the person with whom you live.<br><br>I am angry Matt because he's the most selfish prick/bastard you've ever seen! It's not until it's too late that he realizes he acts in a stupid way. He lies most of the time (<i>dare I say all the times?</i>), he knows it but it's like he can't do anything about it. He is in self-destruction mode.<br> <blockquote>
  <i>
    <b> Happiness is useless to me</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br>I yelled at Hannah so much and I wanted to shake her so bad!. Everything she does, she does to protect Matt, out of love for him. Even when he tells her he loves her writing more she managed to be satisfied<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1415031782i/11718458._SY540_.jpg" width="369" height="467" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>I wanted to slap him countless times. The more he told lies and the more I wanted to hit him!<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1415031782ra/11718459.gif" width="400" height="225" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>But my little heart relented in the end. Once again thanks to M.Pierce I don't completely hate Matt <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ I liked how Matt doesn't fall in his old patterns. Although he's unhappy Hannah's gone, he knows he's responsible. He managed to stay calm, to act less impulsively . After much thought and after talking with several people, this is how we see the evolution of his character  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> And all this leads to predict a good third book which I hope will reveal us more on Matt.<br><br>Oh but Matt:<br><img src="https://p.gr-assets.com/540x540/fit/hostedimages/1384405615/6869506.gif%20" width="400" height="225" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <i>Final thought </i>
</b><br><br>Regardless of whether or not you liked this book, I am sure you will sometimes feel extreme emotions, and just for that, I tip my hat to the author. Because basically, what do you want when you read a book. We want to be transported to another reality, we want out of our lives, we want to dream. But we also want to feel emotions of any kind. So just for that, I say to M.Pierce, well done! <br><br><b>One more (little) request</b><br><br>M.Pierce if you read this, I know you don't plan to make a spinoff (I read it on Facebook) but pretty pretty please, can you make a little exception for Seth?<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1491877624ra/22456923.gif" width="400" height="216" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I think he deserves his own happiness and I really want to read it. I think I may be in love with him. Thank you <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1399929453ra/9611123.gif" width="400" height="160" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Meet Matt and Hannah: <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/20646604.Night_Owl__Night_Owl___1_" title="Night Owl (Night Owl, #1) by M. Pierce" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1394385445s/20646604.jpg" alt="Night Owl (Night Owl, #1) by M. Pierce" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br>Third book <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/20944389.After_Dark__Night_Owl___3_" title="After Dark (Night Owl, #3) by M. Pierce" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1394751725s/20944389.jpg" alt="After Dark (Night Owl, #3) by M. Pierce" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <b>release date : 03/24/15</b><br><br><b> ~Posted before writing my review ~</b><br>The Jury is still undecided on what to think about this book!<br><br> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1414683939ra/11677390.gif" width="400" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Sure I felt a lot of emotions. I've never screamed so much at my Ipad (poor thing) and I almost DNF the book but no like a good girl I keep reading and <s>honestly I don't know if I should have.</s> <i>
  <b> scratch that... 1-2 hours after reading I'm glad I finished it because when you feel so much while reading something it must be good.</b>
</i>I liked the ending but I don't see where this book goes for book 3.<br><br>I'll rate and write my review after a few days. I need time to process...</["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer11321483277777020307"><s>2.5 <b>Round and Around and Fucking Around We Go</b> Stars</s><br/><br/>I changed my mind, so it would be:<br/><br/>3.881 <b>I-Was-Bored-then-Intrigued-then-Worried-then-Amazed-then-Pissed-Off-and-then-Ohhh???</b> Stars<br/><br/><s>*migraine is fucking torturing me atm, but I will try to find some time to torture you guys with my review later on*</s><br/><br/>This rant will be short because..am currently on an energy diet.   <span id="freeText11321483277777020307" style="display:none"><s>2.5 <b>Round and Around and Fucking Around We Go</b> Stars</s><br /><br />I changed my mind, so it would be:<br /><br />3.881 <b>I-Was-Bored-then-Intrigued-then-Worried-then-Amazed-then-Pissed-Off-and-then-Ohhh???</b> Stars<br /><br /><s>*migraine is fucking torturing me atm, but I will try to find some time to torture you guys with my review later on*</s><br /><br />This rant will be short because..am currently on an energy diet. (Just like a normal diet, except that instead of not eating much, I am not using my energy much) So here's to failing miserably at that!<br /><br />This book isn't a perfect 5 stars book (or 10, or 100) but it was bearable. I am still alive atm, so it's definitely not a boring-to-<b>death</b> kind of read too. It's more like a you-gotta-be-patient-at-first-before-it-starts-dropping-bombs-here-and-there kind of book. So my advice is, read it, and try not to die due to the boredom at the beginning of the book, and then enjoy it.<br /><br />Damn, I just wrote a manual of How to Read Last Light up there. So much for going fucking simple *shakes head*<br /><br />::: ATTENTION PLEASE! ::: This is where you shoukd stop reading my review if you don't want to be attacked by lots of (I think) minor spoilers.<br /><br />So my thoughs in points would be... (not that people really bother reading this boring part lol)<br /><br />~ the whole he-was-dead thingie kinda felt ri-dick-culous because it was a tad bit over the top for me but hey, people do weird things all the time!<br /><br />~ Melanie. I loved her despite the fact that I don't think the author put her there to be loved. Tbh I have no idea why she actually existed. Hmm..<br /><br />~ Seth. I loved him too. I wonder why he was portrayed as a bad guy when the truth is he was just a cute lil guy with a crush on a bitch. Oops, I mean on Hannah.<br /><br />~ Nate. This one I'm not sure whether to like, to hate or to be blank-face about. Why the visit to the zoo??? Okay, thats a pretty random question but I just don't know where to fit that question in this supposed-to-be-short review. <br /><br />~ Matt. He was still the old Matt, lusting over Hannah 24/7. He made a mistake in his scare-Hannah-off-and-she-will-run-to-him plan, but it's not that bad. It's not like he killed somebody to have Hannah (hmm maybe this is slightly untrue...)<br /><br />~ Hannah. She started okay and then I hated her. The <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[telling Matt that she fucked Seth when it wasn't true just to drive him away ( and then trying to fuck Seth for real just to forget him ) <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> were pretty bitchy of her. I. Just. Couldn't. Accept. It. And she dared to be pissed off when that pissed Matt off. You dont have that right, bitch!<br /><br />And the ending? I was shouting NOOOOOOOOOOO don't do it Matt, don't <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ marry that cheating bitch! but I doubt he would listen to me though lol<br /><br />Okay I am done with my rant. Go on read it and feel my passionate hatred for Hannah too!<br /><br />*damn it, this rant was supposed to be simple!* <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span></span>

<div id="review_1922294639" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1922294639" />
    <a title="Vasiliki" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/32039736-vasiliki"><img alt="Vasiliki" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1454678710p2/32039736.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1922294639?book_show_action=true">Feb 24, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Vasiliki" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Vasiliki" href="/user/show/32039736-vasiliki">Vasiliki</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="ebook 9781466862531" href="/book/show/21805617-last-light">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1922294639" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5074778078488336696">4.25!<br/><br/>After the epilogue of Night Owl, I needed to read immediately Last Light. The scenarios created in my head were driving me crazy until I started reading and found out what exactly happened.<br/><br/>I am really confused about this series. Although the writing is fantastic and it provokes tons of emotions, the story is too difficult to accept. My soul and heart ached during Night Owl and Last Light. Well, this book made me to feel but it wasn’t pleasant, it was a torture. The story is said again by du</span>
  <span id="freeText5074778078488336696" style="display:none">4.25!<br /><br />After the epilogue of Night Owl, I needed to read immediately Last Light. The scenarios created in my head were driving me crazy until I started reading and found out what exactly happened.<br /><br />I am really confused about this series. Although the writing is fantastic and it provokes tons of emotions, the story is too difficult to accept. My soul and heart ached during Night Owl and Last Light. Well, this book made me to feel but it wasn’t pleasant, it was a torture. The story is said again by dual POV that changes with each chapter.<br /><br />Hannah is standing better on her feet. She finally has a life that she likes and goes for it. She loves Matt with all her heart but she refuses to make the choice he wants. I have enormous respect for her. I don’t know if I could have her strength in a similar situation. And she takes the blow and deals with everything thrown at her in the best possible way. By loving him. This is true love! I cannot believe that true love could hurt that much and Hannah was hurt again and again. I don’t know how to explain that Hannah may accepted the ugly -at least for me- behavior of Matt but she wasn’t a doormat for him. She had an opinion and she was voicing it whenever she had the chance.<br /><br />Matt, oh Matt. I still don’t like him. I was really angry with him during this book. I hate that he uses his love to excuse his manipulation and lies! I hate that he can feel lonely and seek company but Hannah may not. I hate that Hannah loves him so much that I cannot stand it when he is away from her in this book. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ And I cannot accept him lying so much and cheating on her for a second time. It wasn’t a physical cheating but emotional cheating is as bad in this case!  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> And the worse part for me is that Hannah can understand him where I honestly can't! She doesn't agree with him but she does understand. I’ve never felt like this for a hero before. It’s shocking for me. <br /><br />Their interactions were perfectly balanced with love and lust. Their discussions weren’t deep or even honest from both sides but their actions said more than words could say. There were so many actions that I couldn’t accept and/or understand. There were events that were just confusing for me. And still, I couldn’t put this book down. I needed to know what happened.<br /><br />The end of this book was abrupt. I was reading about Hannah and Matt and suddenly it stopped. Maybe it was a cliffhanger, maybe it was exactly the point to stop like this. I really don’t know. What I know is that I need time before starting the next installment of this love story. There is pain in love and I need a break from it for now but I will definitely read the end of the story of Hannah and Matt.</span>
  <a data-text-id="5074778078488336696" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
